# Vehicle Weapon System: reflected C++ API

This page documents the supported reflected API that is intended for vehicle setup, Blueprint access, and C++ integration. Names and macro specifiers match the public headers. Internal, legacy-only, deprecated, and experimental members are intentionally omitted.

<div class="api-reference-summary"><span>25 types</span><span>289 UPROPERTY</span><span>116 UFUNCTION</span></div>

## Core components and configuration types

Expand a type to inspect its public properties and functions.

<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>UWeaponSystemComponent</code><small>74 UPROPERTY · 83 UFUNCTION</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>Vehicle-level cache and router for aim channels. The component owns configured axis solving, continuous muzzle traces, and optional ballistic prediction. It does not fire weapons or apply damage; existing camera/AimCube logic submits its selected targets and may consume the compact compatibility caches during migration.</p>
<div><code>UCLASS(ClassGroup = (Vehicles), meta = (BlueprintSpawnableComponent, DisplayName = &quot;Vehicle Weapon System&quot;))</code><span>Header: <code>TurretSystemRuntime/Public/WeaponSystemComponent.h</code></span></div>
</div>

</details>
<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>UTurretControllerComponent</code><small>17 UPROPERTY · 11 UFUNCTION</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>Blueprint-friendly owner for one independent yaw/pitch pair. The initial implementation is intentionally calculation-only: it caches a shadow solution but never rotates a component, writes legacy variables, or sends network traffic. This makes it safe to add to an existing vehicle and compare against its current authoritative turret implementation.</p>
<div><code>UCLASS(ClassGroup = (Vehicles), meta = (BlueprintSpawnableComponent, DisplayName = &quot;Turret Axis Controller (Advanced)&quot;))</code><span>Header: <code>TurretSystemRuntime/Public/TurretControllerComponent.h</code></span></div>
</div>

</details>
<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>UWeaponMuzzleComponent</code><small>15 UPROPERTY · 3 UFUNCTION</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>Passive Blueprint-friendly definition for one logical weapon muzzle. It resolves a component/socket and calculates a world ray, but never traces, fires, rotates, ticks, or replicates.</p>
<div><code>UCLASS(ClassGroup = (Vehicles), meta = (BlueprintSpawnableComponent, DisplayName = &quot;Weapon Muzzle (Advanced)&quot;))</code><span>Header: <code>TurretSystemRuntime/Public/WeaponMuzzleComponent.h</code></span></div>
</div>

<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>UWeaponSystemConfigurationAsset</code><small>6 UPROPERTY</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>Reusable vehicle weapon-system preset. Applying a profile copies its universal axes, installations, and weapons to a Vehicle Weapon System component. A vehicle may preserve its local component/socket bindings while importing the shared behavior settings.</p>
<div><code>UCLASS(BlueprintType, meta = (DisplayName = &quot;Vehicle Weapon System Profile&quot;))</code><span>Header: <code>TurretSystemRuntime/Public/WeaponSystemConfigurationAsset.h</code></span></div>
</div>

## Blueprint value types used by the API

Expand a type to inspect its public properties and functions.

<details class="api-type">
<summary>
<span><code>FTurretAimTarget</code><small>6 UPROPERTY</small></span>
<i aria-hidden="true"></i>
</summary>
<div class="api-type__intro">
<p>World-space command produced by a camera, sight, AimCube, AI controller, or any other aiming source. Point mode preserves parallax for blocking hits; direction mode avoids extremely distant fake endpoints when nothing is hit.</p>
<div><code>USTRUCT(BlueprintType)</code><span>Header: <code>TurretSystemRuntime/Public/TurretSystemTypes.h</code></span></div>
</div>

## Reflection macro guide

<div class="api-macro-grid">
<article><code>UCLASS</code><p>Registers a UObject-derived class with Unreal reflection. Class metadata controls how the component appears in the editor.</p></article>
<article><code>USTRUCT</code><p>Registers a reflected value type. BlueprintType makes the struct usable as a Blueprint pin and variable type.</p></article>
<article><code>UPROPERTY</code><p>Registers a field for serialization, editor exposure, garbage collection, replication, or Blueprint access according to its specifiers.</p></article>
<article><code>UFUNCTION</code><p>Registers a callable or query function. BlueprintCallable, BlueprintPure, and CallInEditor define where it is exposed.</p></article>
<article><code>GENERATED_BODY</code><p>Injects the code generated by Unreal Header Tool. It must remain inside every reflected class or struct.</p></article>
<article><code>EditAnywhere / VisibleAnywhere</code><p>Controls whether a property is editable or only visible in Details.</p></article>
<article><code>BlueprintReadWrite / BlueprintReadOnly</code><p>Controls whether Blueprint graphs can write the property or only read it.</p></article>
<article><code>Category / meta</code><p>Organizes the editor UI and supplies display names, tooltips, conditions, units, clamps, and advanced-display rules.</p></article>
</div>
